# Prepend ourselves to /etc/hosts
grep -w 'local.bltdemo3.com' /etc/hosts || {
  if grep -w '^127\.0\.1\.1' /etc/hosts ; then
    sed -i'' 's/^127\.0\.1\.1\s.*$/127.0.1.1\tlocal.bltdemo3.com\tlocal/' /etc/hosts
  else
    sed -i'' '1i 127.0.1.1\tlocal.bltdemo3.com\tlocal' /etc/hosts
  fi
}

# Update mailname
echo 'local.bltdemo3.com' > /etc/mailname
